a)","village_lgd":"458930","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Asauni","village_lgd":"458966","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Bachharwara","village_lgd":"459018","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Bakulaha","village_lgd":"458944","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Balgaha","village_lgd":"459063","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Bamhaur","village_lgd":"459035","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Bamhori","village_lgd":"459100","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Bamurha","village_lgd":"459124","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Bamurha(Devendranagar)","village_lgd":"459020","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Bamurhiya","village_lgd":"459004","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Bandhaura","village_lgd":"458965","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Bandhur","village_lgd":"459031","panchayat_lgd":"","block_lgd":"3931","total_eligible_population":null,"total_sicklecell_screening_completed":null},{"village_name":"Ba
